    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer17284353965745076845">Jeramiah Poe isn’t just any character in the Realm of Fiction; he is Muse Master—Destiny Diviner—Mysterious Miskriat. Being of neither the Traditional Genre Provinces nor Independent, Poe enjoys an eternal lease on life, so long as his Scribbler keeps him out of publication. <br/><br/>Poe meets Kane, a seven-year-old boy from the Independent Horror Province, where he learns ancient </span>
  <span id="freeText17284353965745076845" style="display:none">Jeramiah Poe isn’t just any character in the Realm of Fiction; he is Muse Master—Destiny Diviner—Mysterious Miskriat. Being of neither the Traditional Genre Provinces nor Independent, Poe enjoys an eternal lease on life, so long as his Scribbler keeps him out of publication. <br /><br />Poe meets Kane, a seven-year-old boy from the Independent Horror Province, where he learns ancient codes are being broken and the horror that should be an act, is real. <br /><br />But the evil clutching Octava is not new and Seven Arks have been sent to Earth to stop it. Only something has gone wrong and Poe is commissioned as the 8th Ark of Octava to discover what has become of the Seven. <br /><br />But his passage to Earth comes with revelations he's not prepared for. Not only does his Scribbler not know of his existence, he's a she that his human form seems allergic to. Poe soon realizes that with each Ark he locates, his powers grow along with his feelings for the Scribbler. And the enemy will try and use both to gain control of the two realms.</span>

<div id="review_1208815510" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1208815510" />
    <a title="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12941902-relentlessbookchic-ramblings-reviews"><img alt="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464483219p2/12941902.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1208815510?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " class="user" itemprop="url" name="RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews " href="/user/show/12941902-relentlessbookchic-ramblings-reviews">RelentlessBookChic Ramblings &amp; Reviews </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24688501-the-scribbler-guardian">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1208815510" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7661539125475589200">I just finished reading this for the second time, why you ask? Because I was trying to figure out how to put into words how I felt about this book. Expletives...lots of expletives would be needed. Did you love Chronicles of Narnia? The NeverEnding Story? Alice in Wonderland? If you love those fantasy worlds with vibrant characters, Heroes and villains then you will love Arks of Octava. Let this fantasy world appease your inner child while the steamy scenes satisfy your adult fascinations! <br/><br/>Let me</span>
  <span id="freeText7661539125475589200" style="display:none">I just finished reading this for the second time, why you ask? Because I was trying to figure out how to put into words how I felt about this book. Expletives...lots of expletives would be needed. Did you love Chronicles of Narnia? The NeverEnding Story? Alice in Wonderland? If you love those fantasy worlds with vibrant characters, Heroes and villains then you will love Arks of Octava. Let this fantasy world appease your inner child while the steamy scenes satisfy your adult fascinations! <br /><br />Let me start by saying that fantasy is not where my heart lies when reading but I was so swept up in this book I could not put it down! I think every author has a signature and one of the many signatures of Lucian is his insane ability to write his characters. He makes those characters come to life and we all become endeared with each and every one of them. <br /><br />Let me introduce you to some of the characters....<br /> <br />Jeremiah Poe is the main man Master Muse Rider from Octavia. He is a perfect mixture of serious, funny, protective and badass hot guy all rolled into one. His ramblings had me in a fit of laughter throughout quite a bit of the book. <br /><br />Kane, cute amazing kid from the Horror province who Poe becomes very protective of. When Poe learns that Kane is experiencing real pain in Octava it leads them on a trip to Earth to find the other Arks and on the doorstep of one Scribbler who will steal both of their hearts. <br /><br />Scribbler (Charlotte) is a funny character as well. Bane did an amazing job capturing the mind of a writer and bringing it to life with her. She and Poe have one thing in common..they both think romance and love are ridiculous but you have to see what happens when changes start to take place. Do they learn to love each other? Do they fight it tooth and nail and give you a very entertaining book? <br /><br />So Arks of Octava has something for everyone. The kid in you wanting to take a journey to another world. The Adult who wants the steamy alpha male. The hopeless romantic wishing for the HEA for everyone. There is action, suspense, sex, drama and this story paints the most vivid of pictures in your mind while you read. I could see the beautiful music from the Sound Arks, the lights pouring from their instruments while Kane gave it his all as the conductor. I always say I know I have read a really good book when I can see the movie in my head..this was a fantastic movie! <br /><br />My favorite quote from the book: <br /><br /><blockquote>"Because of you, Contessant Juliet, I know life. I know pain. I know pleasure," he barely managed the hot rasp. "I know real." He lowered and kissed her trembling lips with a near hallowed reverence."I know the greatest love in all the realms. Because I know you."</blockquote><br /><br />Relentlessbookchic approved and recommended! <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7661539125475589200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_1183965777" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1183965777" />
    <a title="Mary Strunk" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14526256-mary-strunk"><img alt="Mary Strunk" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1421595326p2/14526256.jpg" /></a>

  <span id="freeText362503439499208366" style="display:none"><strong>Amazing Read</strong><br /><br />I loved this book. This is my first fantasy story that I read and I'm so happy that I did. If I could give this more than 5 stars I would. I was hooked from the beginning and felt like I was getting to know all the characters as I meet them. So much happens thru out the book and the emotions that you have, oh I cried in some parts. <br /><br />This story will take you on a trip to where you will read about each character and what their story is. Poe &amp; Scribbler's journey will keep you going and not wanting it to end. You shall face the battles with them and understand each puzzle piece. <br /><br />Great job to the author on another amazing book. I look forward to more of this series. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4046602641541903409">Arks of Octavia <br/><br/>My Review<br/><br/>So I have been promoting this book for weeks now and really never read the synopis or anything about it lol. So when I started reading I didnt really know what I was getting into. I am a huge fan of Lucian Bane , so I knew whatever he wrote I would love.   <span id="freeText4046602641541903409" style="display:none">Arks of Octavia <br /><br />My Review<br /><br />So I have been promoting this book for weeks now and really never read the synopis or anything about it lol. So when I started reading I didnt really know what I was getting into. I am a huge fan of Lucian Bane , so I knew whatever he wrote I would love. I have never really been into the fantasy or paranormal genres, but Lucian Bane has changed that. First with Ruin and now with Arks of Octavia. This book was AMAZING!!! It was the best book I have read by far this year. This is a very heart warming story. This story is unlike any you will ever read. The emotianal journey these characters go through is fantastic. The way they connect and interact together was so entertaining. I laughed and cried so much. It is such an original concept. Kane is an amazing kid and the true hero in this story. I can't ever remember loving a character as much as I love Kane. Mr. Poe and his scribbler's relationship evolves so great. I love the way they interact and come together. Their love in the end is so magical. This is a must read. It's one of the few 5 star ratings I give out. Love, love, love this book. Can't wait for the next one!!!</span>

Kane &amp; Poe are all part of Octava. Its exciting, dangerous, but believe me no matter what I say here it will not do this fantastic book justice, you will have to read it yourself to understand why this is such a fantastic book.<br /><br />The Author has created a masterpiece, totally different from anything I have ever read, very different from anything he has written before, but he mastered it to perfection. </span>

  <span id="freeText9801414202228280236" style="display:none">Whoa!!!<br /><br />If you are familiar with author Lucian Bane then you will know that this master piece of fanstasy meets reality is sooooo not the Lucian Bane we know and love!<br /><br />That being said I have just read and am absolutely astounded at this mans writing ability.           <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24688501-the-scribbler-guardian">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1204379938" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9285006079187761687">5 out of 5 Stars!<br/><br/>While reading the blurbs and excerpts leading up to the book's release, I admit to being seriously confused as to what it was about. So, while I wasn't sure what to expect, 7% in, I know what I got - “Hill-Derky-Derk-Bomb-Pow”– pure genius!<br/><br/>The entire literary world is “brought to life” in “The Arks of Octava”. Genres, tropes, plots and characters each have been used to world-build the kingdom of Octava, and the results are phenomenal! <br/><br/>Octava is in the Scribbler's Realm, where ch</span>
  <span id="freeText9285006079187761687" style="display:none">5 out of 5 Stars!<br /><br />While reading the blurbs and excerpts leading up to the book's release, I admit to being seriously confused as to what it was about. So, while I wasn't sure what to expect, 7% in, I know what I got - “Hill-Derky-Derk-Bomb-Pow”– pure genius!<br /><br />The entire literary world is “brought to life” in “The Arks of Octava”. Genres, tropes, plots and characters each have been used to world-build the kingdom of Octava, and the results are phenomenal! <br /><br />Octava is in the Scribbler's Realm, where characters written into existence by scribblers (writers/authors) exist while not being scribbled for. Jeremiah Poe, The Great Muse Rider, Changer of Lives and Definer of Destinies, and a Guardian, lives in Octava. He is also a Miskriat – a character who exists only in his Scribbler's mind, with no story written for him yet. So while he was a defined character, his story was not, and therein lies the source of his power (energy). Other story beings from various provinces (genres) approach him for help from time to time concerning matters outside of their storyline.<br /><br />Befriending a small, scared boy, Kane, he found wandering in the Horror Province, is what leads Poe to actually step into a story to help the child. Kane and other children are being hurt INSIDE their stories – something that is expressly forbidden in Octava. Poe will have to travel outside the realm...to Earth...to retrieve the Seven Arks, to end the injustice. This also brings him face to face with his creator...his Scribbler, J.P. Howe – a woman - Charlotte!<br /><br />There is quite a bit of fun...and confusion, as Poe and Charlotte figure out who they are, what is real, and how to go about finding the Seven Arks. Poe also has to deal with feelings, emotions and doubt for the first time in his short existence as coming to 'earth has made him human. Although she is human, Charlotte has to deal with the same issues, having blocked them out long ago and sequestered herself away in near isolation to write under a variety of pen names.<br /><br />There is an evil chasing them as they begin their journey. An evil that does not want the revelations found out on Earth returned to Octava. Poe and Charlotte have to contend with the evil forces at hand, the lost memories of each found Ark...and each other.<br /><br />The avid reader, and the passionate writer will devour this tale with glee! Lucian Bane has taken the strands of literature and woven them into a mesmerizing story that is “unputdownable!”<br /><br />The story does not end in book 1, but there isn't really a cliffhanger – I hate those – but more a pause to regroup...and get ready.<br /><br />“Arks of Octava: The Scribbler Guardian” is considered a Fantasy Romance, but I guarantee that no matter what your genres of preference are, you will enjoy this book!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9285006079187761687" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText15184821227918758144" style="display:none">An AMAZING fantasy adventure!<br /><br />This story sucked me in from start to finish. Even if I wasn’t already a fan of Lucian Bane’s books, this one would have sealed the deal. The story comes alive almost the instant you begin to read. I HIGHLY recommend this book for ANYONE who truly wants to feel connected to a story that has them craving more.<br /><br />I look forward to the future installments for this trilogy &amp; I hope he finds a way to branch off from this particular tale, as I just can’t seem to get enough of it!</span>

  <span id="freeText11302144720235717781" style="display:none">I’ve been wanting to read a book by this author for years. After a recommendation by a Goodreads friend I chose this one and dug in. And holy heck! It was freaking amazing!<br /><br />This was everything I needed in a fantasy romance and so much more. I loved the other worldly feel of Octava as well as Poe’s reactions and thoughts regarding the various characters and areas found there. This has a touch of humor, immense steam, mystery and drama. And then the very best of endings, considering it ends on a cliffhanger which I despise but was so glad to run off of, bringing a dark danger into this fantastical world. <br /><br />There are no words to describe this book except unique in the very best of ways and with a true love story that took me completely by surprise with the emotions it wrought within me. I will definitely be reading the next book and highly recommend this for anyone wanting a great fantasy read that is completely original in every way.<br /><br />Dual POV<br />Safe <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[no ow/om drama; H has actually never been with a woman – but he is a character in a book and designed to negate anything resembling romance; h not a virgin  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />Triggers <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[no apparent triggers although some of the characters have had horrendous pasts – no details  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1343494094" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6756613929782705273">don't even know where to start with The Scribbler Guardian. I finished this book three days ago and I'm still trying to wrap my brain around everything....or pick up the pieces of my heart may be more like it! Total book hangover!!<br/><br/>First, I shall say that I'm an avid reader, reading about one book a day for the last 15 years with many before that, so in total I've read thousands. Never have i felt so emotional with one!<br/>I'm not going to tell you the synopsis of the book as I'm sure that's already </span>
  <span id="freeText6756613929782705273" style="display:none">don't even know where to start with The Scribbler Guardian. I finished this book three days ago and I'm still trying to wrap my brain around everything....or pick up the pieces of my heart may be more like it! Total book hangover!!<br /><br />First, I shall say that I'm an avid reader, reading about one book a day for the last 15 years with many before that, so in total I've read thousands. Never have i felt so emotional with one!<br />I'm not going to tell you the synopsis of the book as I'm sure that's already been explained plenty. So I'll just tell MY experience with it and how it made me feel.<br />I've read some fantasy but have to admit, that fantasy is usually not my favorite genre. Nothing wrong with it, its just never been my preference. But I was totally blown away and swallowed whole from the first page of the Scribbler Guardian!<br />Watching Poe and Kane bond in a magical mystical world of fiction, I could only envision the amazing surroundings of Octava! Bane's description and his ability to color the world of my imagination is indescribable! I wanted to jump tight ibto the book just so I could explore Octava! By 15% of the way in the book I was already attached to Poe and Kane.<br />I couldn't sleep as I witnessed the awkward introduction of Charlotte into the story and than began to slowly follow her attraction and pull to Poe as a lover and Kane as a son. The feelings of confusion Poe felt throughout his stay in reality had me feeling bad for him and trying to understand by placing myself in his shoes. In many ways, he was like a child just learning about life.<br />I never lost interest in this book as we followed the adventure of collecting the Ark's, watching in my head as the story unfolded. Many times I could not put the book down and fell asleep with my glasses on while reading! Every chapter I read led me to more questions of which I hope I will be answered further in the series. My theories on why things happened and how people relate in the book changes the further I got into the book.<br />By the last few chapters my heart was in my throat. And at the end I sobbed like an emotional woman on her period watching sad commercials!!<br />Full out cryfest with tears flowing, snotty nose , hiccupping all the way to the finish! I could see and feel Charlotte's love for Kane and Poe and my heart was ripped straight from my chest right along with her!!<br />Bane has the innate ability to very slowly pull you into his books. He wraps his descriptive fingers around your throat and before you know it your crying, sobbing and confused as to whether you want to finish because you don't want to leave the fictional world hes placed you in! Lucian knows how to write all over my heart with the scribble of his pen or the type of his fingers on a computer!! He will forever be one of my favorite authors and the The Scribbler Guardian has quickly surpassed every book I've read to become one of my very favorite reads!!!<br />So jump right in...a great adventure awaits!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="6756613929782705273" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10379139290608454992">I'll admit. I'm not a fantasy fan. However, I am a Lucian fan and wanted to give Scribbler a fair shot. WOW! Was I blown away! At first, I was wondering what was happening, but it all started to come together and Mr. Bane turned me into a believer of this wonderful and unique fantasy.<br/><br/>The plot of this book was genius in my opinion. Charlotte is a very well known author (scribbler) whose hero, Jeremiah Poe, comes to life and knocks on her door. She created him to be her perfect man...a brawny, goo</span>
  <span id="freeText10379139290608454992" style="display:none">I'll admit. I'm not a fantasy fan. However, I am a Lucian fan and wanted to give Scribbler a fair shot. WOW! Was I blown away! At first, I was wondering what was happening, but it all started to come together and Mr. Bane turned me into a believer of this wonderful and unique fantasy.<br /><br />The plot of this book was genius in my opinion. Charlotte is a very well known author (scribbler) whose hero, Jeremiah Poe, comes to life and knocks on her door. She created him to be her perfect man...a brawny, good looking, hero who has NO interest in romance. What happens to him when he and his vitally important little sidekick, Kane, comes to the realm of his scribbler and discovers he has human qualities that he does not understand?<br /><br />There were parts in this book where I laughed out loud... when Poe discovered his...well, I'll leave that for you to read and enjoy for yourself!<br /><br />What the Scribbler doesn't know is that Poe protects the provinces of the genres (horror, romance, paranormal etc). He comes to her world to save his world, Octava. However, there is someone, or something trying to stop them from saving it.<br /><br />There were so many twists and turns and deep meaning behind the plot and behind each word and each character in this book...I would use the word majestic to describe it. The words towards the end of the book projected a crystal clear picture of a miraculous scene. I would love to see what it would look like in a movie...however, I still don't think it would be as beautiful in a movie than it was in words.<br /><br />This is definitely a book that I would recommend and I can NOT wait until the 2nd book comes out!</span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1451309602441894593">Characters are real in this fantastical story from an author's imagination of a alternate realm of possibilities. The Muse-Rider, Mr. Poe is an unfinished character in an abandoned story, but in the fictional world he lives in he can do incredible tricks, amazing and very powerful things.   <span id="freeText1451309602441894593" style="display:none">Characters are real in this fantastical story from an author's imagination of a alternate realm of possibilities. The Muse-Rider, Mr. Poe is an unfinished character in an abandoned story, but in the fictional world he lives in he can do incredible tricks, amazing and very powerful things. His journey, along with Kane, take you on a trick of the mind and muse as they attempt to help the world of Octava. Nothing is as it seems, and everything can be rewritten with the power of WORDS!<br />I don't know how Mr. Bane does it...but I believe that was his best book I've read yet....I'm in tears having finished and absolutely feel the fear and love in this book. So moving and just overwhelmingly heartfelt emotions throughout....can't wait to follow more of Poe, Kane, and his Scribblers journey!<br />A definite MUST read, any reader, author, lover of books, and scribbler should make this book a priority read! Yes it's that good!!</span>

    <a title="Tanya Rae ~ TaSTy WordGasms" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/21289746-tanya-rae-tasty-wordgasms"><img alt="Tanya Rae ~ TaSTy WordGasms" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557335984p2/21289746.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1201985326?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tanya Rae ~ TaSTy WordGasms" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tanya Rae ~ TaSTy WordGasms" href="/user/show/21289746-tanya-rae-tasty-wordgasms">Tanya Rae ~ TaSTy WordGasms</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24688501-the-scribbler-guardian">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21289746-tanya-rae-tasty-wordgasms?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/21289746-tanya-rae-tasty-wordgasms?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1201985326" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer148279504316980749">Well this is a hard review for me because Arks of Octava - The Scribbler Guardian is a Fantasy Romance and is definitely a different genre than what I have read before. I thought it was a great concept. Scribblers writing the stories and there is a scribbler for each genre, Horror, Paranormal, Romance, Fantasy, etc. The characters acting out what the Scribblers write about.<br/><br/>I had a hard time following the story and felt it was very convoluted. I wish there was a kind of road map to the characters</span>
  <span id="freeText148279504316980749" style="display:none">Well this is a hard review for me because Arks of Octava - The Scribbler Guardian is a Fantasy Romance and is definitely a different genre than what I have read before. I thought it was a great concept. Scribblers writing the stories and there is a scribbler for each genre, Horror, Paranormal, Romance, Fantasy, etc. The characters acting out what the Scribblers write about.<br /><br />I had a hard time following the story and felt it was very convoluted. I wish there was a kind of road map to the characters to keep all the characters straight. I had to create my own so I started highlighting all the genres and then who the ARKs and Scribblers were. Just to try to help me follow the story.<br /><br />There is a little cliffhanger at the end so beware but, you know there will be more…… so the story continues! I have a feeling we will see more of Poe, Juliet and Kane! As well as some of the other characters. I give Arks of Octava 3.5 stars.<br /><br />This ARC was received for an honest review.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9345253371093382619">Lucian does it again. I was completely taken with this story. Kane, Poe, The Scribbler were written with such care. Poe not liking to be touched, his Scribbler not writing romance and Kane with his keen ability to solve the puzzles so quickly. There was sadness with how Kane had been treated, guilt from Poe's Scribbler with her writing, and humor when Poe had to take time out to go to the bathroom. In the end these characters learned how to feel, to have trust and to love. The path they traveled</span>
  <span id="freeText9345253371093382619" style="display:none">Lucian does it again. I was completely taken with this story. Kane, Poe, The Scribbler were written with such care. Poe not liking to be touched, his Scribbler not writing romance and Kane with his keen ability to solve the puzzles so quickly. There was sadness with how Kane had been treated, guilt from Poe's Scribbler with her writing, and humor when Poe had to take time out to go to the bathroom. In the end these characters learned how to feel, to have trust and to love. The path they traveled was truly exquisite. Lucian never fails to take us on a journey that encapsulates us in the world he has created. I love the quirkiness of this story and cannot wait to follow this amazing creation of fantasy and reality. Ineffable as always Lucian!<br /></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1395993094" />
    <a title="Jan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16162673-jan"><img alt="Jan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440446005p2/16162673.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1395993094?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jan" href="/user/show/16162673-jan">Jan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1395993094" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11523189959421219769"><strong>THE SCRIBBLER GUARDIAN IS SPELLBINDING!!!!!</strong><br/><br/>I have to begin by saying that this book is on my list of top ten best reads EVER! It doesn't fit neatly into any specific genre box for me, but it has elements from several genres that combine to make it an incredibly unique story that completely captivated me from the first page to the last! <br/><br/><br/>What is it that makes The Scribbler Guardian so unique? First, the setting of Octava is so fantastical, or is it really? Hmmmm, just one of the many questions fro</span>
  <span id="freeText11523189959421219769" style="display:none"><strong>THE SCRIBBLER GUARDIAN IS SPELLBINDING!!!!!</strong><br /><br />I have to begin by saying that this book is on my list of top ten best reads EVER! It doesn't fit neatly into any specific genre box for me, but it has elements from several genres that combine to make it an incredibly unique story that completely captivated me from the first page to the last! <br /><br /><br />What is it that makes The Scribbler Guardian so unique? First, the setting of Octava is so fantastical, or is it really? Hmmmm, just one of the many questions from the story that kept me wondering. Next, the characters, they are so tangible. No, wait! This is fiction, they can't be real! Well, maybe just the Scribbler? But I love Poe and Kane and they felt real to me! Poe and his Scribbler, well they.........didn't they? Another uncertainty. Ok, so the plot, that should be easy to pin down and describe, right? Which plot though? There were several of them carefully woven throughout the story that just kept adding more layers and depth and more inquiry. I love a book that keeps me off-balance! <br /><br /><br /> So, to sum it up, The Scribbler Guardian is most definitely a creative masterpiece that kept me totally engaged in living the story alongside these amazing characters, taking their unpredictable journey with them, and loving every minute of it! Well played Mr. Bane! Thanks for sharing your creative genius with us again!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11523189959421219769" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1206788188" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1206788188" />
    <a title="Terrie Meerschaert" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16005981-terrie-meerschaert"><img alt="Terrie Meerschaert" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1357140450p2/16005981.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1206788188?book_show_action=true">Feb 20, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Terrie Meerschaert" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Terrie Meerschaert" href="/user/show/16005981-terrie-meerschaert">Terrie Meerschaert</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1206788188" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9871663997918386079">What a wild ride! Just when I thought I was getting used to being in Octava with Mr. Poe and Kane, they were torpedoed into life on Earth as humans. Did I mentioned Octava is a fictional place and all the characters there are fictional. Mr. Poe is in search of his Scribbler to help him find the way to save people in Octava, like Kane, from being abused and hurt. Their quest takes them on a journey like no other and love rules the day!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1390750765" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1390750765" />
    <a title="Ellie Masters" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8173023-ellie-masters"><img alt="Ellie Masters" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598629633p2/8173023.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1390750765?book_show_action=true">Sep 13, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ellie Masters" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ellie Masters" href="/user/show/8173023-ellie-masters">Ellie Masters</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8173023-ellie-masters?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1390750765" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17906334774716989098">Well, hot damn! That was a FRESH and wonderfully crafted tale. I had to spend a few days to formulate my thoughts on this one, figuring out how to put into words the FEELINGS marked into my heart and seeped into my soul after travelling in, and then out, of Poe’s universe. What sort of book was this? Well, it’s a mix of fantasy, adventure, and a sprinkling of romance thrown in as a wonderful and unexpected surprise.<br/><br/>If you love a good fantasy, and a story where the boundaries between worlds colli</span>
  <span id="freeText17906334774716989098" style="display:none">Well, hot damn! That was a FRESH and wonderfully crafted tale. I had to spend a few days to formulate my thoughts on this one, figuring out how to put into words the FEELINGS marked into my heart and seeped into my soul after travelling in, and then out, of Poe’s universe. What sort of book was this? Well, it’s a mix of fantasy, adventure, and a sprinkling of romance thrown in as a wonderful and unexpected surprise.<br /><br />If you love a good fantasy, and a story where the boundaries between worlds collide, then this is the take-me-away-adventure for you. The story reminds me of children walking through a wardrobe and stumbling into a magical world where a lion is king, of a precious girl sliding down a rabbit hole where nothing is what it seems, or a land where the magic of dreams comes alive for a boy and his flying ‘dog?’<br /><br />In the Scribbler Guardian, heroes are front and center and the villains are very real, and oh so malevolent, yet understated in such a way as to make them even more vile. Such vibrant characters come to life in this book, it makes you stop … PAUSE … and go ‘Wait…could this in fact be real?’ Is it happening now?<br /><br />That is the true wonder behind the gifted storytelling on these pages … The magic of this book is once you’re a few chapters in, you may just begin to believe the very premise behind the entire captivating world. As a novelist myself, I know I will never again write the same way again. The characters speaking to me to write their stories have always been alive to me, but now they have a home…PRECISELY BECAUSE OF THIS BOOK! They are ALIVE and BREATHE within the world of Octava.<br /><br />So, let’s talk about some of those characters… <br /><br />Let’s speak about Jeremiah Poe, the Master Muse Rider, a character who remains true to his Scribbler’s incarnation from beginning to end, and yet even then is capable of an intensity of growth and self-expression. He is a protector, a badass in his creation, he takes his role seriously, and endowed with the physical attributes of an alpha male, imbued with incredibly powerful sex appeal…an unexpected side effect of his Scribbler when he was created. Poe tackles his task with a single-minded determination, never once wavering from his goal, even when faced with an impossible and unwanted ending. He defends those weaker than himself, and it is in his interactions with the supporting characters where we see the soul created for Jeremiah Poe truly shine. His innocence is real. His sexiness is off the charts hot. The combination makes for some seriously explosive scenes.<br /><br />Jeremiah Poe had me in awe from page one through the end, and yet there was another who stole the show from time to time. Kane, a cute and amazing genius-child from the Horror Province, brings all of Poe’s protective instincts to the forefront. When Poe learns Kane is experiencing true, horrific acts within his story, pain that shouldn’t be real in Octava, Poe is led on a journey to save this wonderful child.<br /><br />The journey Poe and Kane take leads them directly to Poe’s creator, his Scribbler, a god-like figure who he reveres. Charlotte, a wonderfully funny and flawed woman, has one thing in common with the character she created but never finished writing. They both hate the messiness of romance… which sets up a wonderful romantic subplot to follow. For a woman who despises all things feminine and a man who believes love is a contagion, the path the two of them travel is wonderfully creative and magnificent, and steamy, dreamy, hot.<br /><br />And, yet, there is a bad guy out there…and Poe is on a quest, one he cannot accomplish without the aid of Kane. Charlotte helps too; assisting Poe and Kane in their search, she navigates the foreign landscape of Earth. The three of them work together…most of the time.<br /><br />The Scribbler Guardian has something for everyone … Fantasy … Adventure … Romance … Humor … a touch of Horror … and tons of fun. I felt transported into another realm. The kid in me enjoyed the fantasy. The hopeless romantic fawned over the steamy alpha male, and the action adventurer cheered the team closer to the final goal…<br /><br />I would highly recommend this FIVE STAR book!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17906334774716989098" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1213230173" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1213230173" />
    <a title="Amanda Miller /A Bookaholic&#39;s Fix: Feeding the Addiction" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3450346-amanda-miller-a-bookaholic-s-fix-feeding-the-addiction"><img alt="Amanda Miller /A Bookaholic&#39;s Fix: Feeding the Addiction" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420488942p2/3450346.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1213230173?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Amanda Miller /A Bookaholic&#39;s Fix: Feeding the Addiction" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Amanda Miller /A Bookaholic&#39;s Fix: Feeding the Addiction" href="/user/show/3450346-amanda-miller-a-bookaholic-s-fix-feeding-the-addiction">Amanda Miller /A Bookaholic&#39;s Fix: Feeding the Addiction</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/24688501-the-scribbler-guardian">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1213230173" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3549883986514206169">I guess I have hit a bit of a good luck streak with the books I've read recently. This one is another brilliant, five-star, perfect 10 read. It may seem that I give away good scores but trust me, I am a very discriminate reader and I cannot give top marks to a book that doesn't earn it.<br/><br/>Time for me to explain exactly how this book earned such a high rating.<br/><br/>First, there was the premise of the story. The idea that the fictional characters created by the world's authors live in another realm is intr</span>
  <span id="freeText3549883986514206169" style="display:none">I guess I have hit a bit of a good luck streak with the books I've read recently. This one is another brilliant, five-star, perfect 10 read. It may seem that I give away good scores but trust me, I am a very discriminate reader and I cannot give top marks to a book that doesn't earn it.<br /><br />Time for me to explain exactly how this book earned such a high rating.<br /><br />First, there was the premise of the story. The idea that the fictional characters created by the world's authors live in another realm is intriguing to say the least. I loved how these characters lived and operated withing the parameters of the stories they were created to tell but also interact with characters from other stories. Poe's reputation as the Muse Rider and the duties that entailed were pure genius. I have often heard authors tell how their original plans for a story have been altered by their characters--unruly creations who didn't like their fates--hell, I have encountered this phenomenon in my own writing. The idea that a creation would have the power to change the fates of other characters... absolutely incredible! I also loved the idea of crossing over from the fictional realm to the real one. (Kinda like the movie Pagemaster- only in reverse!)<br /><br />Then there was the style of the story. The beginning of the book was different. The language was a bit pretentious and sometimes difficult to follow. (I will give the cold I was battling some credit for having me a bit addled to begin with.) I will admit that I was a bit worried that the entire book would be ostentatious but as Poe's character interacted with others (especially Kane), he became more human and his thoughts and speech became much easier to follow. (Even though I sill liken him to Ichabod Crane from the Sleepy Hollow series.) You may wonder how I didn't find fault with this fact... Well, I have an explanation. You see, the period of difficulty didn't last long. In fact, as the story started to form, the character morphed. I equated it with the writing process- the first draft seems rigid, the character apathetic, but then as the author develops the story, more facets of the character become evident. I believe that the portion I had difficulty was written that way intentionally. Another thing that made me think this was done deliberately was the picnic scene. Poe changed the fate of a character in a romance and during the picnic he and Kane had with the girl and her parents, her name changes--it is Isabelle in most places and yet she is called Susan at least twice. It made me think that by changing her fate, he may have inadvertently changed other things about her within her own story. The thought-provoking aspect of the style had me itching to drag out my old go-tos and start analyzing the story.<br /><br />I liked the characters and loved the bond that formed between them. I enjoyed the story-line--it was unique and compelling. The story flowed well--the action was great, the sex fit in with the story. And most importantly, it left me wanting to find out more about this fascinating world. Bravo Lucian Bane, you have my attention. I will be waiting for the next installment.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3549883986514206169" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

		<td>
		    <b>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('v/my7o6qsMIcUUPH0ZsrDhAz5QcCqs+QkdYfDvq9DJghAMtW11XNPf4qsaPZ1PYYZv40+TU5n9QsFWtUAyHRyg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('PC8MxIN67/np/b52ksGF0eqBWTyjl4yOWRSzmnAZdUWi1nV82oWSBguGTBKajljHnEyIwpQE3Mrk18fAiYWoFw==')})
  }

All of Mackenzie’s late husbands were millionaires. Each died suddenly and quite mysteriously of massive heart attacks (in spite of no history of heart trouble). And every time, they vow to get their due—with no consequence. But this time is different.
